# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
2x2 matrix ... stop after reach 2^2 (4) visits ^Qy6FpBEE

- start at r0,c0
- inc col till length-1
- inc row till length-1
- dec col till it
  reaches start idx
- dec row till it reaches start idx+1
- visits_counter should
  equal length square;
  thus we reached the end.
  -  If not then inc col by 1, keep row same; dec length by 1; optionally check bounds;
     NOTE: we have new values for start row_idx and col_idx; recurse;; ^b4Ocj7Cq

REPEAT ^sYqlvQSm

visits_counter == length^2 ^zrONRuqx

length = 4

r0 c0
r0 c1
r0 c2
r0 c3
r1 c3
r2 c3
r3 c3
r3 c2
r3 c1
r3 c0
r2 c0
r1 c0
r1 c1
r1 c2
r2 c2
r2 c1 ^Q0VbJhLy

visits_counter != length^2
length -= 1; col+= 1; continue ^SZtjVbdY

static ^e7f0dtAR

visits_counter == length^2 ^4aXmgBrd

r0 c0
r0 c1
r0 c2
r0 c3
r0 c4
r1 c4
r2 c4
r3 c4
r4 c4
r4 c3
r4 c2
r4 c1
r4 c0
r3 c0
r2 c0
r1 c0 visits_counter != length^2
r1 c1 new_length = 4
r1 c2
r1 c3
r2 c3
r3 c3
r3 c2
r3 c1
r2 c1 visits_counter != length^2
r2 c2 new_length = 3
visits_counter == length^2 ^hQI7qKaI

THIS IS THE BASE CASE FOR RECURSION
should be checked  first thing! ^3LbjXB7c
